 'I am born a Hindu, but i will not die a Hindu' Ambedkar was able to unite and empower them politically and socially to empower the Dalits, with the same strength that their opponents also prevent them Were pushing for lambey sangharsh ke baad jab ambedkar ko bharosa ho gaya ki ve hindu dharm se jatipratha or chuaa-chhot kii kureetiyaan dur nahin kar paa rahe to unhone wo aitihaasik vaktavy diya, jisamen unhone kaha ki main hindu paidaa to hua hum, lekin hindu maruunga nahin
 22 pledges to initiate Buddhism Protest on Hindu Code Bill After independence, Dr
 Ambedkar became Law Minister in Nehru's cabinet and on Nehru's initiative he prepared the Hindu Code Bill, but he also had to face strong opposition to this bill

 Adopted Buddhism: In 1956 Ambedkar, along with his 3,80,000 companions, converted to Hinduism and converted to Buddhism
 1950 ke dashak main hi baba sahib buddha dharm ke prati aakarshith hue or buddha sammelan main bhaag lene srilanka (tab ceylone) gaye

 mahaan sant devraha baba kii dharti devaria loksabhaa kshetra uttar pradesh ke 80 sansadeey siton main se ek he or isaki sansadeey sankhya 66 he
 The history of Deoria is very old
 mana jaataa he ki devaria naam kii utpatti ‘devarany’ yaa ‘devpuria’ se hui thi
 According to official figures, the name 'deoria' is derived from its headquarters and means a place where there are many temples
 devaria jila uttar pradesh ke purvi kshetra main sthit he

 yahaan par lambey samay tak congress kaa dabadabaa rahaa

 vah 1952 se 57 tak pehle loksabhaa main yahaan kaa pratinidhitiv kiya

 yahaan se rajmangal pandey bhi (1984 or 1989) saansad rahe

 - maa ganga mahadev kii jataaon main nivas karti hai
 - Ganges bathing, worshiping and darshan eliminates sins and liberates from diseases
 - jo tirth ganga kinare based hue hai

 kai prayaason ke baad bhi vigyaan ganga jal ke gunon kaa sahi-sahi rahasy nahin jaan paaya

 - ganga nadi kaa jal saalon tak prayog karne or rakhane par bhi kharaab nahin hota
 - Regular use of Ganga water cures diseases
 - haalanki ganga ke in gunon ke rahasy se log bahut had tak anjaan hai
 - Some people call it miracle, some people associate it with herbs and Ayurveda
 - vigyaan bhi iske divine or chamatkaari gunon ko sweekaar karata he
 - In the spirituality world it can be called a miracle of positive energy

 menopause tab hota he, jab mahilaon kii overi yaa andashay main estrogen or projesterone naam ke hormone banane band ho jate hai

 25 June
 
 
 
 a day that changed the direction of Indian sports in terms of Indian cricket
 25 june 1983 ko aaj ke hi din kapildev ke ranvankuron ne behad shaktishaalee westeindies team ko 43 ran se haraakar worldcup champion banane kaa gaurav hasil kiya tha
 Later in the year 2011, Mahendra Singh Dhoni repeated this feat by defeating Sri Lanka in the final

 With this charismatic victory, Indian cricket made the world realize its power for the first time
 is jeet ke baad hi bhartiya cricketron par khub dhan kii barish hui or desh main cricket ko peshewar game kaa darja mila
 Today, even in a T20 match in the short-form format, it is common to score around 200 and even 250 runs, but in the 80s it was a big thing to score more than 200 in ODI cricket
 aaj ke daur ke cricket prashansakon ko yah jaankaar hairat ho sakati he ki tab ke 60-60 over ke vanade match main bhartiya team ne mahaj 183 ran kaa score banaaya tha or 43 ran ke achche khaas antar se jeet liya tha
 The final will also be remembered for a memorable catch by legendary all-rounder Kapil Dev for West Indies great batsman Viv Richards
 england main yojit pehle teen worldcup 60-60 over ke hue
 The West Indies team, who were champions in the first two World Cups, were once again in the finals in 1983 and they were facing a very weak Indian team
 us daur kii indies team ke khel kaushal kaa loha puri duniya maanati thi

 View this post on instagramrepost from @wildcraftin So here goes the story behind this
 Since childhood, whenever i used to visit the north and central part of Calcutta essentially, i would feel sympathetic everytime i would spot a hand pulled rickshaw, thereby choosing not to use them
 Until recently when my sympathy coincided with the realization that we're helping to earn their bread and butter only when we're taking a ride
 So last time i was in Calcutta, the # wildcraftwildling in me decided to pull a handpull rickshaw instead, to see how difficult and strenuous it really is
 i asked the rickshaw uncle to have a seat while i pulled him around on the streets of Shobhabazar, tickling the bell at intervals while the whole street stood and watched in awe
 i realized though there's a lot of mechanism involved, it wasn't a piece of cake at all
 All my years of inquistiveness transpired to salutation for the extreme precision and relentless efforts that go in during each trip made
 Yet each day they wake up with the same enthusiasm to battle the odds
 This spirit is what inspires me to be # readyforanything
